# ✅ Chinese Textbook Vocabulary — Expanded (Sentences & Tags)

*Aligned with [ChineseVocab.md](./ChineseVocab.md) — Speak Chinese Together 1 (一起说中文1), Lessons 1-24*

# ✅ Lesson 1 — You, Me and Him (Expanded)

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |
|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|
| 你 | nǐ | you (2nd person singular) | 1. 你好吗？<br>Nǐ hǎo ma?<br>How are you?<br>2. 你是学生吗？<br>Nǐ shì xuésheng ma?<br>Are you a student? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 是 | shì | be (am/is/are) | 1. 我是老师。<br>Wǒ shì lǎoshī.<br>I am a teacher.<br>2. 他是我的朋友。<br>Tā shì wǒ de péngyou.<br>He is my friend. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:grammar` `hsk:1` |
| 中国 | Zhōngguó | China | 1. 我来自中国。<br>Wǒ láizì Zhōngguó.<br>I come from China.<br>2. 中国很大。<br>Zhōngguó hěn dà.<br>China is very big. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:countries` `hsk:1` |
| 中国人 | Zhōngguórén | Chinese (person) | 1. 她是中国人。<br>Tā shì Zhōngguórén.<br>She is Chinese.<br>2. 我不是中国人。<br>Wǒ bú shì Zhōngguórén.<br>I am not Chinese. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:nationality` `hsk:1` |
| 吗 | ma | [used at the end of an interrogative sentence] | 1. 你是老师吗？<br>Nǐ shì lǎoshī ma?<br>Are you a teacher?<br>2. 这是你的书吗？<br>Zhè shì nǐ de shū ma?<br>Is this your book? | `type:particle` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:grammar` `hsk:1` `grammar:question particle` |
| 我 | wǒ | I; me | 1. 我是学生。<br>Wǒ shì xuésheng.<br>I am a student.<br>2. 这是我的手机。<br>Zhè shì wǒ de shǒujī.<br>This is my phone. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 老师 | lǎoshī | teacher | 1. 他是我的老师。<br>Tā shì wǒ de lǎoshī.<br>He is my teacher.<br>2. 老师，你好！<br>Lǎoshī, nǐ hǎo!<br>Hello, teacher! | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:school,people` `hsk:1` |
| 不 | bù | no; not | 1. 我不是学生。<br>Wǒ bú shì xuésheng.<br>I am not a student.<br>2. 她不是中国人。<br>Tā bú shì Zhōngguórén.<br>She is not Chinese. | `type:adverb` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:grammar` `hsk:1` |
| 学生 | xuésheng | student | 1. 我是学生。<br>Wǒ shì xuésheng.<br>I am a student.<br>2. 他们是我的学生。<br>Tāmen shì wǒ de xuésheng.<br>They are my students. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:school,people` `hsk:1` |
| 他 | tā | he; him | 1. 他是谁？<br>Tā shì shéi?<br>Who is he?<br>2. 他是我的老师。<br>Tā shì wǒ de lǎoshī.<br>He is my teacher. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 谁 | shéi | who | 1. 这是谁？<br>Zhè shì shéi?<br>Who is this?<br>2. 谁是你的老师？<br>Shéi shì nǐ de lǎoshī?<br>Who is your teacher? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:questions` `hsk:1` `grammar:question word` |
| 我的 | wǒ de | my; mine | 1. 这是我的书。<br>Zhè shì wǒ de shū.<br>This is my book.<br>2. 那是我的手机。<br>Nà shì wǒ de shǒujī.<br>That is my phone. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:possession` `hsk:1` |
| 这 | zhè | this | 1. 这是我的书。<br>Zhè shì wǒ de shū.<br>This is my book.<br>2. 这是谁？<br>Zhè shì shéi?<br>Who is this? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 你们 | nǐmen | you (2nd person plural) | 1. 你们好！<br>Nǐmen hǎo!<br>Hello everyone!<br>2. 你们是学生吗？<br>Nǐmen shì xuésheng ma?<br>Are you (all) students? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 书 | shū | book | 1. 这是我的书。<br>Zhè shì wǒ de shū.<br>This is my book.<br>2. 那本书是你的吗？<br>Nà běn shū shì nǐ de ma?<br>Is that book yours? | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:objects,school` `hsk:1` |
| 我们 | wǒmen | we; us | 1. 我们是学生。<br>Wǒmen shì xuésheng.<br>We are students.<br>2. 这是我们的书。<br>Zhè shì wǒmen de shū.<br>This is our book. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 那 | nà | that | 1. 那是你的手机吗？<br>Nà shì nǐ de shǒujī ma?<br>Is that your phone?<br>2. 那是我的朋友。<br>Nà shì wǒ de péngyou.<br>That is my friend. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |
| 你的 | nǐ de | your; yours (2nd person singular) | 1. 这是你的书吗？<br>Zhè shì nǐ de shū ma?<br>Is this your book?<br>2. 那是你的朋友。<br>Nà shì nǐ de péngyou.<br>That is your friend. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:possession` `hsk:1` |
| 手机 | shǒujī | mobile phone | 1. 那是你的手机吗？<br>Nà shì nǐ de shǒujī ma?<br>Is that your phone?<br>2. 我的手机在这儿。<br>Wǒ de shǒujī zài zhèr.<br>My phone is here. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:electronics` `hsk:1` |
| 朋友 | péngyou | friend | 1. 这是我的朋友。<br>Zhè shì wǒ de péngyou.<br>This is my friend.<br>2. 她是我朋友的朋友。<br>Tā shì wǒ péngyou de péngyou.<br>She is my friend's friend. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:relationships` `hsk:1` |
| 她 | tā | she; her | 1. 她是谁？<br>Tā shì shéi?<br>Who is she?<br>2. 她是我的朋友。<br>Tā shì wǒ de péngyou.<br>She is my friend. | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson1` `frequency:high` `topic:pronouns` `hsk:1` |

# ✅ Lesson 2 — I Come to China to Learn Chinese (Expanded)

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |
|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|
| 去 | qù | go to | 1. 你去学校吗？<br>Nǐ qù xuéxiào ma?<br>Are you going to school?<br>2. 我去中国学习汉语。<br>Wǒ qù Zhōngguó xuéxí Hànyǔ.<br>I'm going to China to study Chinese. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:movement` `hsk:1` |
| 学校 | xuéxiào | school | 1. 我去学校。<br>Wǒ qù xuéxiào.<br>I'm going to school.<br>2. 这是一所大学校。<br>Zhè shì yī suǒ dà xuéxiào.<br>This is a big school. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:school` `hsk:1` |
| 对 | duì | right; correct | 1. 对，我去学校。<br>Duì, wǒ qù xuéxiào.<br>Right, I'm going to school.<br>2. 你说得对。<br>Nǐ shuō de duì.<br>You're right. | `type:adjective` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:agreement` `hsk:1` |
| 会 | huì | can | 1. 你会说汉语吗？<br>Nǐ huì shuō Hànyǔ ma?<br>Can you speak Chinese?<br>2. 我会说英语。<br>Wǒ huì shuō Yīngyǔ.<br>I can speak English. | `type:verb (modal)` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:ability` `hsk:1` `grammar:modal verb` |
| 说 | shuō | speak; say | 1. 你会说汉语吗？<br>Nǐ huì shuō Hànyǔ ma?<br>Can you speak Chinese?<br>2. 请慢慢说。<br>Qǐng mànmàn shuō.<br>Please speak slowly. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:communication` `hsk:1` |
| 汉语 | Hànyǔ | Chinese (language) | 1. 我会说汉语。<br>Wǒ huì shuō Hànyǔ.<br>I can speak Chinese.<br>2. 我来中国学习汉语。<br>Wǒ lái Zhōngguó xuéxí Hànyǔ.<br>I came to China to study Chinese. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:language` `hsk:1` |
| 写 | xiě | write | 1. 我不会写汉字。<br>Wǒ bú huì xiě Hànzì.<br>I can't write Chinese characters.<br>2. 请写拼音。<br>Qǐng xiě pīnyīn.<br>Please write it in Pinyin. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:writing` `hsk:1` |
| 汉字 | Hànzì | Chinese character | 1. 我不会写汉字。<br>Wǒ bú huì xiě Hànzì.<br>I can't write Chinese characters.<br>2. 这个汉字怎么读？<br>Zhège Hànzì zěnme dú?<br>How do you read this character? | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:language` `hsk:1` |
| 来 | lái | come | 1. 你来中国做什么？<br>Nǐ lái Zhōngguó zuò shénme?<br>What did you come to China to do?<br>2. 我来学习汉语。<br>Wǒ lái xuéxí Hànyǔ.<br>I came to study Chinese. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:movement` `hsk:1` |
| 做 | zuò | do | 1. 你来中国做什么？<br>Nǐ lái Zhōngguó zuò shénme?<br>What did you come to China to do?<br>2. 你在做什么？<br>Nǐ zài zuò shénme?<br>What are you doing? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:actions` `hsk:1` |
| 什么 | shénme | what | 1. 你叫什么名字？<br>Nǐ jiào shénme míngzi?<br>What is your name?<br>2. 你想做什么？<br>Nǐ xiǎng zuò shénme?<br>What do you want to do? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:questions` `hsk:1` `grammar:question word` |
| 学习 | xuéxí | study; learn | 1. 我来中国学习汉语。<br>Wǒ lái Zhōngguó xuéxí Hànyǔ.<br>I came to China to study Chinese.<br>2. 学习汉语很有意思。<br>Xuéxí Hànyǔ hěn yǒuyìsi.<br>Learning Chinese is very interesting. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:education` `hsk:1` |
| 看 | kàn | see; read; look at | 1. 你看什么书？<br>Nǐ kàn shénme shū?<br>What book are you reading?<br>2. 我看汉语书。<br>Wǒ kàn Hànyǔ shū.<br>I'm reading a Chinese book. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:actions` `hsk:1` |
| 请问 | qǐngwèn | excuse me | 1. 请问，你叫什么名字？<br>Qǐngwèn, nǐ jiào shénme míngzi?<br>Excuse me, what's your name?<br>2. 请问这个字怎么读？<br>Qǐngwèn zhège zì zěnme dú?<br>Excuse me, how is this character read? | `type:verb phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:polite expressions` `hsk:1` |
| 怎么 | zěnme | how | 1. 这个汉字怎么读？<br>Zhège Hànzì zěnme dú?<br>How do you read this character?<br>2. 这个用汉语怎么说？<br>Zhège yòng Hànyǔ zěnme shuō?<br>How do you say this in Chinese? | `type:pronoun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:questions` `hsk:1` `grammar:question word` |
| 读 | dú | pronounce; read | 1. 请跟我读。<br>Qǐng gēn wǒ dú.<br>Please read after me.<br>2. 这个汉字怎么读？<br>Zhège Hànzì zěnme dú?<br>How do you pronounce this character? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:reading` `hsk:1` |
| 爱 | ài | love | 1. 我爱看书。<br>Wǒ ài kàn shū.<br>I love reading.<br>2. 我爱我的家人。<br>Wǒ ài wǒ de jiārén.<br>I love my family. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:emotions` `hsk:1` |
| 生词 | shēngcí | new word | 1. 这个生词是什么意思？<br>Zhège shēngcí shì shénme yìsi?<br>What does this new word mean?<br>2. 今天有很多生词。<br>Jīntiān yǒu hěn duō shēngcí.<br>There are many new words today. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:language,school` `hsk:2` |
| 意思 | yìsi | meaning | 1. 这个生词是什么意思？<br>Zhège shēngcí shì shénme yìsi?<br>What does this new word mean?<br>2. 我不懂这个意思。<br>Wǒ bù dǒng zhège yìsi.<br>I don't understand this meaning. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:language` `hsk:1` |
| 想 | xiǎng | want | 1. 我想学习汉语。<br>Wǒ xiǎng xuéxí Hànyǔ.<br>I want to learn Chinese.<br>2. 你想知道什么？<br>Nǐ xiǎng zhīdào shénme?<br>What do you want to know? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:desire` `hsk:1` `grammar:modal verb` |
| 知道 | zhīdào | know | 1. 我想知道你的名字。<br>Wǒ xiǎng zhīdào nǐ de míngzi.<br>I want to know your name.<br>2. 我不知道。<br>Wǒ bù zhīdào.<br>I don't know. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:cognition` `hsk:1` |
| 听 | tīng | listen to | 1. 请听我说。<br>Qǐng tīng wǒ shuō.<br>Please listen to me.<br>2. 我喜欢听音乐。<br>Wǒ xǐhuan tīng yīnyuè.<br>I like listening to music. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:actions` `hsk:1` |
| 拼音 | pīnyīn | Pinyin | 1. 请写拼音。<br>Qǐng xiě pīnyīn.<br>Please write it in Pinyin.<br>2. 拼音帮助我们读汉字。<br>Pīnyīn bāngzhù wǒmen dú Hànzì.<br>Pinyin helps us read Chinese characters. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:language` `hsk:1` |
| 上课 | shàngkè | Class begins! | 1. 上课！大家请坐。<br>Shàngkè! Dàjiā qǐng zuò.<br>Class begins! Everyone please sit.<br>2. 我们八点上课。<br>Wǒmen bā diǎn shàngkè.<br>We start class at 8. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` `grammar:separable` |
| 下课 | xiàkè | Class is over! | 1. 下课！明天见。<br>Xiàkè! Míngtiān jiàn.<br>Class is over! See you tomorrow.<br>2. 下午三点下课。<br>Xiàwǔ sān diǎn xiàkè.<br>Class ends at 3pm. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` `grammar:separable` |
| 休息一下 | xiūxi yíxià | Take a break. | 1. 我们休息一下吧。<br>Wǒmen xiūxi yíxià ba.<br>Let's take a break.<br>2. 休息一下眼睛。<br>Xiūxi yíxià yǎnjing.<br>Rest your eyes for a bit. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` `grammar:verb+一下` |
| 请听我说 | qǐng tīng wǒ shuō | Please listen to me. | 1. 请听我说完。<br>Qǐng tīng wǒ shuō wán.<br>Please listen until I'm finished.<br>2. 老师说：请听我说。<br>Lǎoshī shuō: qǐng tīng wǒ shuō.<br>The teacher said: please listen to me. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 请跟我读 | qǐng gēn wǒ dú | Please read after me. | 1. 请跟我读这个生词。<br>Qǐng gēn wǒ dú zhège shēngcí.<br>Please read this new word after me.<br>2. 大家请跟我读一遍。<br>Dàjiā qǐng gēn wǒ dú yí biàn.<br>Everyone, read after me once. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 请看白板 | qǐng kàn báibǎn | Please look at the whiteboard. | 1. 请看白板上的例句。<br>Qǐng kàn báibǎn shàng de lìjù.<br>Please look at the example sentences on the whiteboard.<br>2. 请看白板，这是今天的语法点。<br>Qǐng kàn báibǎn, zhè shì jīntiān de yǔfǎ diǎn.<br>Look at the whiteboard — here's today's grammar point. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:medium` `topic:classroom` |
| 请看书 | qǐng kàn shū | Please look at the book. | 1. 请看书第五页。<br>Qǐng kàn shū dì-wǔ yè.<br>Please look at page 5 of the book.<br>2. 请看书上的图片。<br>Qǐng kàn shū shàng de túpiàn.<br>Please look at the pictures in the book. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` |
| 请再说一遍 | qǐng zài shuō yí biàn | Please say it again. | 1. 我没听清，请再说一遍。<br>Wǒ méi tīng qīng, qǐng zài shuō yí biàn.<br>I didn't hear clearly, please say it again.<br>2. 请再说一遍你的名字。<br>Qǐng zài shuō yí biàn nǐ de míngzi.<br>Please say your name again. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` |
| 请写拼音 | qǐng xiě pīnyīn | Please write it in Pinyin. | 1. 请写拼音，不要写汉字。<br>Qǐng xiě pīnyīn, bú yào xiě Hànzì.<br>Please write Pinyin, not characters.<br>2. 每个生词请写拼音在旁边。<br>Měi ge shēngcí qǐng xiě pīnyīn zài pángbiān.<br>Please write Pinyin next to each new word. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:medium` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 第几声 | dì jǐ shēng | Which tone? | 1. 这个字第几声？<br>Zhège zì dì jǐ shēng?<br>Which tone is this character?<br>2. "妈"和"麻"的第几声不一样？<br>"Mā" hé "má" de dì jǐ shēng bù yíyàng?<br>Which tones differ between "mā" and "má"? | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` |
| 请慢慢说 | qǐng mànmàn shuō | Please speak slowly. | 1. 请慢慢说，我在记笔记。<br>Qǐng mànmàn shuō, wǒ zài jì bǐjì.<br>Please speak slowly, I'm taking notes.<br>2. 你的汉语太快了，请慢慢说。<br>Nǐ de Hànyǔ tài kuài le, qǐng mànmàn shuō.<br>Your Chinese is too fast, please speak slowly. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 我没听懂 | wǒ méi tīngdǒng | I didn't understand. | 1. 对不起，我没听懂。<br>Duìbuqǐ, wǒ méi tīngdǒng.<br>Sorry, I didn't understand.<br>2. 老师说得太快了，我没听懂。<br>Lǎoshī shuō de tài kuài le, wǒ méi tīngdǒng.<br>The teacher spoke too fast, I didn't understand. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:1` `grammar:resultative complement` |
| 把书翻到第一页 | bǎ shū fāndào dì-yī yè | Turn to page 1. | 1. 请大家把书翻到第一页。<br>Qǐng dàjiā bǎ shū fāndào dì-yī yè.<br>Everyone, turn to page 1.<br>2. 把书翻到第一页，我们开始读课文。<br>Bǎ shū fāndào dì-yī yè, wǒmen kāishǐ dú kèwén.<br>Turn to page 1, let's start reading the text. | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` `grammar:把-sentence` |
| 请问这个用汉语怎么说 | qǐngwèn zhège yòng Hànyǔ zěnme shuō | Excuse me, how do you say this in Chinese? | 1. 老师，请问这个用汉语怎么说？<br>Lǎoshī, qǐngwèn zhège yòng Hànyǔ zěnme shuō?<br>Teacher, excuse me, how do you say this in Chinese?<br>2. 这个水果的名字用汉语怎么说？<br>Zhège shuǐguǒ de míngzi yòng Hànyǔ zěnme shuō?<br>How do you say this fruit's name in Chinese? | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 请问这个汉字怎么读 | qǐngwèn zhège Hànzì zěnme dú | Excuse me, how do you pronounce this Chinese character? | 1. 请问这个汉字怎么读？是第三声吗？<br>Qǐngwèn zhège Hànzì zěnme dú? Shì dì-sān shēng ma?<br>How do you read this character? Is it third tone?<br>2. 这个汉字很难，请问怎么读？<br>Zhège Hànzì hěn nán, qǐngwèn zěnme dú?<br>This character is hard — how do you pronounce it? | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |
| 请问这个生词是什么意思 | qǐngwèn zhège shēngcí shì shénme yìsi | Excuse me, what does this new word mean? | 1. 请问"方便"这个生词是什么意思？<br>Qǐngwèn "fāngbiàn" zhège shēngcí shì shénme yìsi?<br>What does the new word "fāngbiàn" mean?<br>2. 我不懂这个生词，请问是什么意思？<br>Wǒ bù dǒng zhège shēngcí, qǐngwèn shì shénme yìsi?<br>I don't understand this new word — what does it mean? | `type:phrase` `lesson:lesson2` `frequency:high` `topic:classroom` `hsk:2` |

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |

# ✅ Lesson 14 — What Classes Do We Have Today? (Expanded)

|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |
|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|
| 头疼 | tóuténg | have a headache | 1. 我头疼、咳嗽，还有点儿发烧。<br>Wǒ tóuténg, késou, hái yǒudiǎnr fāshāo.<br>I have a headache, a cough, and a slight fever.<br>2. 你头疼吗？<br>Nǐ tóuténg ma?<br>Do you have a headache? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson20` `frequency:high` `topic:health` `hsk:3` |

| 电梯 | diàntī | lift | 1. 电梯在右边。<br>Diàntī zài yòubiān.<br>The elevator is on the right.<br>2. 电梯坏了，我们走楼梯吧。<br>Diàntī huài le, wǒmen zǒu lóutī ba.<br>The elevator is broken, let's take the stairs. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:buildings` `hsk:2` |
| 上去 | shàngqù | go up; [used after a verb, indicating upward movement] | 1. 我们坐电梯上去。<br>Wǒmen zuò diàntī shàngqù.<br>Let's take the elevator up.<br>2. 他上楼去了。<br>Tā shànglóu qù le.<br>He went upstairs. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:movement` `hsk:2` `grammar:directional complement` |
| 把 | bǎ | [used to advance the object of a verb to the position before it] | 1. 把蛋糕放在冰箱里。<br>Bǎ dàngāo fàng zài bīngxiāng lǐ.<br>Put the cake in the refrigerator.<br>2. 把门关上。<br>Bǎ mén guān shàng.<br>Close the door. | `type:preposition` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:grammar` `hsk:2` `grammar:把-sentence` |
| 蛋糕 | dàngāo | cake | 1. 这个蛋糕很好吃。<br>Zhège dàngāo hěn hǎochī.<br>This cake is very tasty.<br>2. 生日蛋糕上插着蜡烛。<br>Shēngrì dàngāo shàng chā zhe làzhú.<br>There are candles on the birthday cake. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:food,celebrations` `hsk:1` |
| 放 | fàng | put; place | 1. 把蛋糕放在冰箱里。<br>Bǎ dàngāo fàng zài bīngxiāng lǐ.<br>Put the cake in the refrigerator.<br>2. 包放在哪儿了？<br>Bāo fàng zài nǎr le?<br>Where did you put the bag? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:actions` `hsk:1` |
| 冰箱 | bīngxiāng | refrigerator | 1. 冰箱里有牛奶。<br>Bīngxiāng lǐ yǒu niúnǎi.<br>There's milk in the refrigerator.<br>2. 把蛋糕放在冰箱里。<br>Bǎ dàngāo fàng zài bīngxiāng lǐ.<br>Put the cake in the refrigerator. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:home,appliances` `hsk:1` |
| 邀请 | yāoqǐng | invite | 1. 他邀请我去他的生日聚会。<br>Tā yāoqǐng wǒ qù tā de shēngrì jùhuì.<br>He invited me to his birthday party.<br>2. 你邀请了多少人？<br>Nǐ yāoqǐng le duōshao rén?<br>How many people did you invite? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:social` `hsk:2` |
| 小区 | xiǎoqū | residential quarter | 1. 我住在一个安静的小区。<br>Wǒ zhù zài yí ge ānjìng de xiǎoqū.<br>I live in a quiet residential area.<br>2. 小区门口有一个超市。<br>Xiǎoqū ménkǒu yǒu yí ge chāoshì.<br>There's a supermarket at the entrance of the community. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:places,home` `hsk:2` |
| 门口 | ménkǒu | doorway; entrance | 1. 我在门口等你。<br>Wǒ zài ménkǒu děng nǐ.<br>I'll wait for you at the entrance.<br>2. 小区门口有一个超市。<br>Xiǎoqū ménkǒu yǒu yí ge chāoshì.<br>There's a supermarket at the entrance of the community. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:location` `hsk:1` |
| 栋 | dòng | [used for housing] | 1. 我们住在一栋楼里。<br>Wǒmen zhù zài yī dòng lóu lǐ.<br>We live in one building.<br>2. 这栋楼有十层。<br>Zhè dòng lóu yǒu shí céng.<br>This building has ten floors. | `type:measure` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:medium` `topic:grammar` `hsk:2` |
| 马上 | mǎshàng | at once; immediately | 1. 我马上到。<br>Wǒ mǎshàng dào.<br>I'll be there right away.<br>2. 电影马上开始了。<br>Diànyǐng mǎshàng kāishǐ le.<br>The movie is about to start. | `type:adverb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:time` `hsk:1` |
| 下来 | xiàlái | come down | 1. 你快下来吧。<br>Nǐ kuài xiàlái ba.<br>Come down quickly.<br>2. 他从楼上下来了。<br>Tā cóng lóu shàng xiàlái le.<br>He came down from upstairs. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:movement` `hsk:2` `grammar:directional complement` |
| 才 | cái | not until | 1. 他十点才来。<br>Tā shí diǎn cái lái.<br>He didn't come until ten o'clock.<br>2. 我吃完饭才做作业。<br>Wǒ chī wán fàn cái zuò zuòyè.<br>I only do homework after finishing dinner. | `type:adverb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:grammar,time` `hsk:2` |
| 发现 | fāxiàn | discover; find | 1. 我发现了一个秘密。<br>Wǒ fāxiàn le yí ge mìmì.<br>I discovered a secret.<br>2. 你发现有什么不同吗？<br>Nǐ fāxiàn yǒu shénme bùtóng ma?<br>Did you notice any difference? | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:perception` `hsk:2` |
| 热情 | rèqíng | enthusiastic | 1. 他很热情地欢迎我们。<br>Tā hěn rèqíng de huānyíng wǒmen.<br>He welcomed us warmly.<br>2. 这位服务员很热情。<br>Zhè wèi fúwùyuán hěn rèqíng.<br>This waiter is very enthusiastic. | `type:adjective` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:personality` `hsk:2` |
| 欢迎 | huānyíng | welcome; greet | 1. 欢迎来我家！<br>Huānyíng lái wǒ jiā!<br>Welcome to my home!<br>2. 大家热烈欢迎新同学。<br>Dàjiā rèliè huānyíng xīn tóngxué.<br>Everyone warmly welcomes the new classmate. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:social` `hsk:1` |
| 点 | diǎn | light (a candle) | 1. 点蜡烛。<br>Diǎn làzhú.<br>Light the candles.<br>2. 他点了一根烟。<br>Tā diǎn le yī gēn yān.<br>He lit a cigarette. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:actions` `hsk:1` |
| 蜡烛 | làzhú | (wax) candle | 1. 生日蜡烛吹灭了。<br>Shēngrì làzhú chuī miè le.<br>The birthday candles were blown out.<br>2. 停电的时候我们点了蜡烛。<br>Tíngdiàn de shíhou wǒmen diǎn le làzhú.<br>When the power went out, we lit candles. | `type:noun` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:medium` `topic:celebrations,home` `hsk:2` |
| 祝 | zhù | express good wishes | 1. 祝你成功！<br>Zhù nǐ chénggōng!<br>Wishing you success!<br>2. 祝你们幸福。<br>Zhù nǐmen xìngfú.<br>Wishing you happiness. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:greetings` `hsk:1` |
| 感动 | gǎndòng | be moved; be touched | 1. 他的故事让我很感动。<br>Tā de gùshi ràng wǒ hěn gǎndòng.<br>His story moved me deeply.<br>2. 收到礼物后她感动得哭了。<br>Shōudào lǐwù hòu tā gǎndòng de kū le.<br>After receiving the gift, she was so moved she cried. | `type:verb/adjective` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:emotions` `hsk:2` |
| 感谢 | gǎnxiè | thank; be grateful | 1. 感谢你的帮助。<br>Gǎnxiè nǐ de bāngzhù.<br>Thank you for your help.<br>2. 我感谢每一位朋友。<br>Wǒ gǎnxiè měi yī wèi péngyou.<br>I am grateful to every friend. | `type:verb` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:emotions,social` `hsk:2` |
| 心里 | xīnlǐ | heart; mind | 1. 我心里很开心。<br>Wǒ xīnlǐ hěn kāixīn.<br>I am very happy in my heart.<br>2. 他说的话让我心里暖暖的。<br>Tā shuō de huà ràng wǒ xīnlǐ nuǎn nuǎn de.<br>His words warmed my heart. | `type:noun (location)` `lesson:lesson24` `frequency:high` `topic:feelings` `hsk:2` |

# 🎯 Bonus Vocabulary Sets (Personal Interests — Not from the Textbook)

*These 8 sets are independent of Speak Chinese Together 1 and cover the user's own interests (computers, making, gaming, painting). Kept separate from the 24 textbook lessons above so the two don't get mixed up again.*

# ✅ Bonus Lesson 1 — Computer Parts & Building PCs (Expanded)

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |
|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|
| 电脑 | diànnǎo | computer | 1. 我的电脑很快。<br>Wǒ de diànnǎo hěn kuài.<br>My computer is very fast.<br>2. 你每天用几个小时电脑？<br>Nǐ měitiān yòng jǐ ge xiǎoshí diànnǎo?<br>How many hours a day do you use the computer? | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:computers` `hsk:1` |
| 组装 | zǔzhuāng | to assemble | 1. 我自己组装了一台电脑。<br>Wǒ zìjǐ zǔzhuāng le yī tái diànnǎo.<br>I assembled a computer myself.<br>2. 组装电脑不难。<br>Zǔzhuāng diànnǎo bù nán.<br>Assembling a PC isn't hard. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 硬件 | yìngjiàn | hardware | 1. 电脑硬件越来越便宜。<br>Diànnǎo yìngjiàn yuè lái yuè piányi.<br>Computer hardware is getting cheaper.<br>2. 你需要升级硬件吗？<br>Nǐ xūyào shēngjí yìngjiàn ma?<br>Do you need to upgrade hardware? | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 中央处理器 | zhōngyāng chǔlǐqì | CPU | 1. 中央处理器是电脑的大脑。<br>Zhōngyāng chǔlǐqì shì diànnǎo de dànǎo.<br>The CPU is the brain of the computer.<br>2. 这个中央处理器性能很强。<br>Zhège zhōngyāng chǔlǐqì xìngnéng hěn qiáng.<br>This CPU has very strong performance. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 显卡 | xiǎnkǎ | graphics card | 1. 我的显卡坏了。<br>Wǒ de xiǎnkǎ huài le.<br>My graphics card is broken.<br>2. 玩游戏需要好显卡。<br>Wán yóuxì xūyào hǎo xiǎnkǎ.<br>You need a good graphics card to play games. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers,gaming` |
| 主板 | zhǔbǎn | motherboard | 1. 所有零件都插在主板上。<br>Suǒyǒu língjiàn dōu chā zài zhǔbǎn shàng.<br>All components plug into the motherboard.<br>2. 这个主板支持DDR5内存。<br>Zhège zhǔbǎn zhīchí DDR5 nèicún.<br>This motherboard supports DDR5 RAM. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 内存 | nèicún | RAM / memory | 1. 十六G内存就够了。<br>Shíliù G nèicún jiù gòu le.<br>16GB of RAM is enough.<br>2. 内存不够用。<br>Nèicún bú gòu yòng.<br>The RAM isn't enough. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 硬盘 | yìngpán | hard drive | 1. 我的硬盘满了。<br>Wǒ de yìngpán mǎn le.<br>My hard drive is full.<br>2. 换一个大硬盘。<br>Huàn yí ge dà yìngpán.<br>Swap for a bigger hard drive. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 固态硬盘 | gùtài yìngpán | SSD | 1. 固态硬盘开机很快。<br>Gùtài yìngpán kāijī hěn kuài.<br>An SSD boots up very fast.<br>2. 我把系统装在固态硬盘上。<br>Wǒ bǎ xìtǒng zhuāng zài gùtài yìngpán shàng.<br>I installed the system on the SSD. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 电源 | diànyuán | power supply | 1. 电源坏了电脑就开不了机。<br>Diànyuán huài le diànnǎo jiù kāi bù liǎo jī.<br>If the PSU breaks, the PC won't turn on.<br>2. 买电源要看功率。<br>Mǎi diànyuán yào kàn gōnglǜ.<br>When buying a power supply, check the wattage. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 机箱 | jīxiāng | computer case | 1. 这个机箱很漂亮。<br>Zhège jīxiāng hěn piàoliang.<br>This case is very pretty.<br>2. 我把主板放进机箱里。<br>Wǒ bǎ zhǔbǎn fàng jìn jīxiāng lǐ.<br>I put the motherboard into the case. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 风扇 | fēngshàn | fan | 1. 风扇噪音很大。<br>Fēngshàn zàoyīn hěn dà.<br>The fan is very loud.<br>2. 机箱里装了三个风扇。<br>Jīxiāng lǐ zhuāng le sān ge fēngshàn.<br>Three fans are installed in the case. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:computers` |
| 散热器 | sànrèqì | heatsink / cooler | 1. 散热器上涂了硅脂。<br>Sànrèqì shàng tú le guīzhī.<br>Thermal paste is applied on the heatsink.<br>2. CPU需要好的散热器。<br>CPU xūyào hǎo de sànrèqì.<br>The CPU needs a good cooler. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:low` `topic:computers` |
| 螺丝刀 | luósīdāo | screwdriver | 1. 用螺丝刀拧螺丝。<br>Yòng luósīdāo níng luósī.<br>Use a screwdriver to turn the screws.<br>2. 十字螺丝刀很常用。<br>Shízì luósīdāo hěn chángyòng.<br>Phillips screwdrivers are very common. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:tools` |
| 插槽 | chācáo | slot | 1. 显卡插在PCIe插槽上。<br>Xiǎnkǎ chā zài PCIe chācáo shàng.<br>The graphics card plugs into the PCIe slot.<br>2. 内存插槽有四个。<br>Nèicún chācáo yǒu sì ge.<br>There are four RAM slots. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:low` `topic:computers` |
| 接口 | jiēkǒu | port | 1. USB接口很方便。<br>USB jiēkǒu hěn fāngbiàn.<br>USB ports are very convenient.<br>2. 这个接口坏了。<br>Zhège jiēkǒu huài le.<br>This port is broken. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 电缆 | diànlǎn | cable | 1. 电缆太短了。<br>Diànlǎn tài duǎn le.<br>The cable is too short.<br>2. 整理电缆可以改善散热。<br>Zhěnglǐ diànlǎn kěyǐ gǎishàn sànrè.<br>Managing cables improves cooling. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:medium` `topic:computers` |
| 开机 | kāijī | to power on | 1. 电脑开不了机。<br>Diànnǎo kāi bù liǎo jī.<br>The PC won't power on.<br>2. 开机以后要输密码。<br>Kāijī yǐhòu yào shū mìmǎ.<br>After powering on, you need to enter the password. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:computers` `grammar:separable` |
| 关机 | guānjī | to shut down | 1. 别忘了关机。<br>Bié wàng le guānjī.<br>Don't forget to shut down.<br>2. 电脑自动关机了。<br>Diànnǎo zìdòng guānjī le.<br>The computer shut down automatically. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:computers` `grammar:separable` |
| 重启 | chóngqǐ | to restart | 1. 更新以后需要重启电脑。<br>Gēngxīn yǐhòu xūyào chóngqǐ diànnǎo.<br>You need to restart after an update.<br>2. 我的电脑卡住了，我重启了一下。<br>Wǒ de diànnǎo kǎ zhù le, wǒ chóngqǐ le yīxià.<br>My PC froze, so I restarted it. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus1` `frequency:high` `topic:computers` |

# ✅ Bonus Lesson 2 — 3D Printing (FDM) (Expanded)

| Hanzi | Pinyin | Definition | Example Sentences | Tags |
|-------|--------|------------|------------------|------|
| 三维打印 | sānwéi dǎyìn | 3D printing | 1. 三维打印可以制造玩具。<br>Sānwéi dǎyìn kěyǐ zhìzào wánjù.<br>3D printing can make toys.<br>2. 我在学习三维打印技术。<br>Wǒ zài xuéxí sānwéi dǎyìn jìshù.<br>I am learning 3D printing technology. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:medium` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 打印机 | dǎyìnjī | printer | 1. 打印机没纸了。<br>Dǎyìnjī méi zhǐ le.<br>The printer is out of paper.<br>2. 这台打印机很慢。<br>Zhè tái dǎyìnjī hěn màn.<br>This printer is very slow. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:high` `topic:printing` `hsk:2` |
| 熔融沉积成型 | róngróng chénjī chéngxíng | FDM | 1. 熔融沉积成型是最常见的三维打印技术。<br>Róngróng chénjī chéngxíng shì zuì chángjiàn de sānwéi dǎyìn jìshù.<br>FDM is the most common 3D printing technology.<br>2. 我的打印机使用熔融沉积成型。<br>Wǒ de dǎyìnjī shǐyòng róngróng chénjī chéngxíng.<br>My printer uses FDM. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 喷嘴 | pēnzuǐ | nozzle | 1. 喷嘴堵住了。<br>Pēnzuǐ dǔ zhù le.<br>The nozzle is clogged.<br>2. 换一个更细的喷嘴。<br>Huàn yí ge gèng xì de pēnzuǐ.<br>Swap to a finer nozzle. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 热床 | rèchuáng | heated bed | 1. 热床可以防止翘曲。<br>Rèchuáng kěyǐ fángzhǐ qiàoqū.<br>The heated bed prevents warping.<br>2. 打印前要把热床调平。<br>Dǎyìn qián yào bǎ rèchuáng tiáopíng.<br>Level the heated bed before printing. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 喷头 | pēntóu | extruder | 1. 喷头温度太高了。<br>Pēntóu wēndù tài gāo le.<br>The extruder temperature is too high.<br>2. 清理喷头里的残留塑料。<br>Qīnglǐ pēntóu lǐ de cánliú sùliào.<br>Clean the leftover plastic in the extruder. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 耗材 | hàocái | filament | 1. 我买了新的耗材。<br>Wǒ mǎi le xīn de hàocái.<br>I bought new filament.<br>2. 哪种耗材最结实？<br>Nǎ zhǒng hàocái zuì jiēshi?<br>Which filament is strongest? | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 聚乳酸 | jùrǔsuān | PLA | 1. 聚乳酸是最常用的材料。<br>Jùrǔsuān shì zuì chángyòng de cáiliào.<br>PLA is the most commonly used material.<br>2. 聚乳酸容易打印。<br>Jùrǔsuān róngyì dǎyìn.<br>PLA is easy to print. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 丙烯腈丁二烯苯乙烯 | bǐngxījīng dīngèrxī běnyǐxī | ABS | 1. 丙烯腈丁二烯苯乙烯比聚乳酸更结实。<br>Bǐngxījīng dīngèrxī běnyǐxī bǐ jùrǔsuān gèng jiēshi.<br>ABS is stronger than PLA.<br>2. 打印丙烯腈丁二烯苯乙烯需要通风。<br>Dǎyìn bǐngxījīng dīngèrxī běnyǐxī xūyào tōngfēng.<br>Printing ABS needs ventilation. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 层高 | cénggāo | layer height | 1. 层高越小打印越慢。<br>Cénggāo yuè xiǎo dǎyìn yuè màn.<br>The smaller the layer height, the slower the print.<br>2. 0.2毫米的层高很常用。<br>0.2 háomǐ de cénggāo hěn chángyòng.<br>0.2mm layer height is very common. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 填充 | tiánchōng | infill | 1. 百分之二十的填充就够了。<br>Bǎi fēn zhī èrshí de tiánchōng jiù gòu le.<br>20% infill is enough.<br>2. 填充密度越高越结实。<br>Tiánchōng mìdù yuè gāo yuè jiēshi.<br>The higher the infill density, the stronger it is. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 支撑 | zhīchēng | support | 1. 悬空的部分需要支撑。<br>Xuánkōng de bùfen xūyào zhīchēng.<br>Overhanging parts need supports.<br>2. 支撑很难拆掉。<br>Zhīchēng hěn nán chāi diào.<br>Supports are hard to remove. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:medium` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 切片软件 | qiēpiàn ruǎnjiàn | slicer software | 1. 把模型导入切片软件。<br>Bǎ móxíng dǎorù qiēpiàn ruǎnjiàn.<br>Import the model into the slicer.<br>2. 切片软件可以设置层高和填充。<br>Qiēpiàn ruǎnjiàn kěyǐ shèzhì cénggāo hé tiánchōng.<br>The slicer can set layer height and infill. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 打印床 | dǎyìn chuáng | print bed | 1. 打印床要干净。<br>Dǎyìn chuáng yào gānjìng.<br>The print bed needs to be clean.<br>2. 模型粘在打印床上了。<br>Móxíng zhān zài dǎyìn chuáng shàng le.<br>The model stuck to the print bed. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 粘附 | zhānfù | adhesion | 1. 第一层的粘附很重要。<br>Dì-yī céng de zhānfù hěn zhòngyào.<br>First layer adhesion is very important.<br>2. 用胶水可以增强粘附。<br>Yòng jiāoshuǐ kěyǐ zēngqiáng zhānfù.<br>Using glue can improve adhesion. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 翘曲 | qiàoqū | warping | 1. 翘曲会导致打印失败。<br>Qiàoqū huì dǎozhì dǎyìn shībài.<br>Warping will cause the print to fail.<br>2. 热床可以减少翘曲。<br>Rèchuáng kěyǐ jiǎnshǎo qiàoqū.<br>A heated bed reduces warping. | `type:noun/verb` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 拉丝 | lāsī | stringing | 1. 拉丝很影响外观。<br>Lāsī hěn yǐngxiǎng wàiguān.<br>Stringing affects the appearance a lot.<br>2. 降低温度可以减少拉丝。<br>Jiàngdī wēndù kěyǐ jiǎnshǎo lāsī.<br>Lowering the temperature reduces stringing. | `type:noun/verb` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 调平 | tiáopíng | leveling | 1. 打印前要先调平。<br>Dǎyìn qián yào xiān tiáopíng.<br>Level the bed before printing.<br>2. 自动调平很方便。<br>Zìdòng tiáopíng hěn fāngbiàn.<br>Auto-leveling is very convenient. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 挤出 | jǐchū | extrusion | 1. 挤出太慢会缺料。<br>Jǐchū tài màn huì quē liào.<br>If extrusion is too slow, there will be under-extrusion.<br>2. 检查挤出是否顺畅。<br>Jiǎnchá jǐchū shìfǒu shùnchàng.<br>Check if extrusion is smooth. | `type:noun/verb` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:low` `topic:3dprinting` |
| 模型 | móxíng | model | 1. 我下载了一个玩具模型。<br>Wǒ xiàzài le yí ge wánjù móxíng.<br>I downloaded a toy model.<br>2. 模型不能悬空太多。<br>Móxíng bùnéng xuánkōng tài duō.<br>The model shouldn't have too many overhangs. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus2` `frequency:medium` `topic:3dprinting` |

| 拉伸 | lāshēn | extrude | 1. 把这个圆拉伸成立方体。<br>Bǎ zhège yuán lāshēn chéng lìfāngtǐ.<br>Extrude this circle into a cube.<br>2. 拉伸的方向很重要。<br>Lāshēn de fāngxiàng hěn zhòngyào.<br>The direction of extrusion is important. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 旋转 | xuánzhuǎn | revolve | 1. 旋转草图可以生成圆柱。<br>Xuánzhuǎn cǎotú kěyǐ shēngchéng yuánzhù.<br>Revolving a sketch creates a cylinder.<br>2. 把曲线旋转360度。<br>Bǎ qūxiàn xuánzhuǎn sānbǎi liùshí dù.<br>Revolve the curve 360 degrees. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:high` `topic:cad,movement` `hsk:2` |
| 扫掠 | sǎolüè | sweep | 1. 用扫掠功能做管道。<br>Yòng sǎolüè gōngnéng zuò guǎndào.<br>Use the sweep function to make a pipe.<br>2. 扫掠需要一条路径和一个轮廓。<br>Sǎolüè xūyào yī tiáo lùjìng hé yí ge lúnkuò.<br>Sweep needs a path and a profile. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 放样 | fàngyàng | loft | 1. 放样可以把两个形状连接起来。<br>Fàngyàng kěyǐ bǎ liǎng ge xíngzhuàng liánjiē qǐlai.<br>Loft connects two shapes together.<br>2. 放样适合做复杂曲面。<br>Fàngyàng shìhé zuò fùzá qūmiàn.<br>Loft is good for complex curved surfaces. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 倒角 | dàojiǎo | chamfer | 1. 给边缘倒角更安全。<br>Gěi biānyuán dàojiǎo gèng ānquán.<br>Chamfering the edge is safer.<br>2. 倒角可以消除锋利边缘。<br>Dàojiǎo kěyǐ xiāochú fēnglì biānyuán.<br>Chamfering removes sharp edges. | `type:verb/noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 圆角 | yuánjiǎo | fillet | 1. 给直角做圆角更美观。<br>Gěi zhíjiǎo zuò yuánjiǎo gèng měiguān.<br>Adding fillets to right angles looks better.<br>2. 圆角可以减少应力集中。<br>Yuánjiǎo kěyǐ jiǎnshǎo yìnglì jízhōng.<br>Fillets reduce stress concentration. | `type:verb/noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 抽壳 | chōuké | shell | 1. 抽壳可以把实心变成空心。<br>Chōuké kěyǐ bǎ shíxīn biàn chéng kōngxīn.<br>Shelling turns a solid body hollow.<br>2. 抽壳厚度设为两毫米。<br>Chōuké hòudù shè wéi liǎng háomǐ.<br>Set shell thickness to 2mm. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 布尔运算 | bù'ěr yùnsuàn | Boolean operation | 1. 布尔运算可以合并或切割物体。<br>Bù'ěr yùnsuàn kěyǐ hébìng huò qiēgē wùtǐ.<br>Boolean operations can combine or cut objects.<br>2. 用布尔运算挖一个洞。<br>Yòng bù'ěr yùnsuàn wā yí ge dòng.<br>Use a Boolean operation to dig a hole. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 合并 | hébìng | union | 1. 把这两个物体合并成一个。<br>Bǎ zhè liǎng ge wùtǐ hébìng chéng yí ge.<br>Union these two objects into one.<br>2. 合并后就不能分开了。<br>Hébìng hòu jiù bùnéng fēn kāi le.<br>After union, they can't be separated. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad` `hsk:3` |
| 减去 | jiǎnqù | subtract | 1. 用A减去B得到孔。<br>Yòng A jiǎnqù B dédào kǒng.<br>Subtract B from A to get a hole.<br>2. 减去多余的部分。<br>Jiǎnqù duōyú de bùfen.<br>Subtract the extra parts. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad,math` `hsk:2` |
| 相交 | xiāngjiāo | intersect | 1. 相交运算只保留重叠部分。<br>Xiāngjiāo yùnsuàn zhǐ bǎoliú chóngdié bùfen.<br>Intersect keeps only the overlapping part.<br>2. 两条线相交于一点。<br>Liǎng tiáo xiàn xiāngjiāo yú yī diǎn.<br>Two lines intersect at one point. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad,math` `hsk:3` |
| 参数 | cānshù | parameter | 1. 修改参数模型会自动更新。<br>Xiūgǎi cānshù móxíng huì zìdòng gēngxīn.<br>Change a parameter and the model updates automatically.<br>2. 参数化设计很方便。<br>Cānshù huà shèjì hěn fāngbiàn.<br>Parametric design is very convenient. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad` |
| 特征 | tèzhēng | feature | 1. 拉伸是一个特征。<br>Lāshēn shì yí ge tèzhēng.<br>Extrude is a feature.<br>2. 每个特征在时间轴上都可以编辑。<br>Měi ge tèzhēng zài shíjiān zhóu shàng dōu kěyǐ biānjí.<br>Every feature can be edited in the timeline. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:high` `topic:cad` `hsk:3` |
| 时间轴 | shíjiān zhóu | timeline | 1. 在时间轴上删除一个特征。<br>Zài shíjiān zhóu shàng shānchú yí ge tèzhēng.<br>Delete a feature in the timeline.<br>2. 时间轴记录了建模步骤。<br>Shíjiān zhóu jìlù le jiànmó bùzhòu.<br>The timeline records the modeling steps. | `type:noun` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:low` `topic:cad` |
| 渲染 | xuànrǎn | render | 1. 加材质然后渲染。<br>Jiā cáizhì ránhòu xuànrǎn.<br>Add materials then render.<br>2. 渲染图看起来像照片。<br>Xuànrǎn tú kàn qǐlai xiàng zhàopiàn.<br>The rendered image looks like a photo. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad,graphics` |
| 导出 | dǎochū | export | 1. 把模型导出为STL文件。<br>Bǎ móxíng dǎochū wéi STL wénjiàn.<br>Export the model as an STL file.<br>2. 导出前检查一下单位。<br>Dǎochū qián jiǎnchá yīxià dānwèi.<br>Check the units before exporting. | `type:verb` `lesson:bonus3` `frequency:medium` `topic:cad` `hsk:3` |
